● Now I have everything. Let me walk through all four deep dives.

  ---
  Deep Dive 1: Audio Pipeline End-to-End

  Here's the complete chain with bugs marked:

  Capture → Send

  Microphone (44.1kHz/48kHz float32)
      ↓ AVAudioEngine inputNode tap (1024 frames)
      ↓ processAudioBuffer()
      ↓   → calculates audioLevel for UI (this part is fine)
      ↓   → convertToPCM16()  ← BUG: no resampling, just float→Int16
      ↓ geminiService.sendAudio(data:)
      ↓   → base64 encode
      ↓   → WebSocket: {"realtime_input": {"media_chunks": [{"mime_type": "audio/pcm;rate=16000", "data": "..."}]}}
      ↓
     Gemini receives 48kHz audio labeled as 16kHz → garbled input

  The fix (what GetStream/LiveKit do):

  Microphone (device native rate)
      ↓ AVAudioEngine inputNode tap
      ↓ AVAudioConverter (deviceRate → 16kHz, float32 → Int16, mono)
      ↓ Send resampled PCM16 data

  You need an AVAudioConverter created once at tap setup time:
  let inputFormat = inputNode.outputFormat(forBus: 0)
  let targetFormat = AVAudioFormat(commonFormat: .pcmFormatInt16,
                                    sampleRate: 16000, channels: 1,
                                    interleaved: false)!
  let converter = AVAudioConverter(from: inputFormat, to: targetFormat)!

  Then in the tap callback, convert each buffer before sending.

  Receive → Playback

  Gemini WebSocket response
      ↓ serverContent.modelTurn.parts[].inlineData.data (base64)
      ↓ Data(base64Encoded:) → raw PCM bytes
      ↓ playAudio(data:)
      ↓   → pendingAudioChunks queue
      ↓   → makePCMBuffer(from:) using playbackFormat
      ↓       playbackFormat = 16kHz  ← BUG: Gemini sends 24kHz
      ↓   → AVAudioPlayerNode.scheduleBuffer()
      ↓
     Plays 24kHz audio at 16kHz → everything sounds slow/deep

  The fix: Change playback format to match Gemini's output:
  let format = AVAudioFormat(commonFormat: .pcmFormatInt16,
                             sampleRate: 24_000, channels: 1,
                             interleaved: false)

  One subtlety: the AVAudioEngine.mainMixerNode may need to resample from 24kHz to the hardware output rate.
  AVAudioEngine handles this automatically when you connect nodes — you just need to specify the correct format on the
  connection.

  What swift-gemini-api does differently

  From the research, their GeminiLiveClient handles:
  - VAD (Voice Activity Detection): Detects when the user stops speaking and automatically marks turn completion. Your
  current implementation relies entirely on Gemini's server-side VAD (which works, but client-side VAD gives snappier
  turn-taking).
  - Audio format abstraction: They encapsulate the PCM format specs so you never mismatch rates.
  - Chunking: They may batch audio frames to reduce WebSocket message overhead (sending every 100ms instead of every
  buffer callback).

  ---
  Deep Dive 2: WebSocket Protocol Details

  Handshake Flow

  Client                              Gemini
    |                                    |
    |──── WebSocket CONNECT ────────────>|
    |<─── WebSocket OPEN ──────────────--|
    |                                    |
    |──── {"setup": {...}} ────────────->|  (model, config, tools, system prompt)
    |<─── {"setupComplete": {}} ────────|  (ready to receive audio)
    |                                    |
    |──── {"realtime_input": {...}} ───->|  (audio chunks, continuous)
    |──── {"realtime_input": {...}} ───->|
    |                                    |
    |<─── {"serverContent": {           |  (multiple messages)
    |        "inputTranscript": "...",   |  (what user said - STT)
    |        "modelTurn": {             |
    |          "parts": [               |
    |            {"inlineData": {...}},  |  (audio response)
    |            {"transcript": "..."}   |  (what AI said - STT of its audio)
    |          ]                         |
    |        },                          |
    |        "turnComplete": true        |  (AI finished speaking)
    |      }}                            |

  Your current setup message (correct structure):

  {
    "setup": {
      "model": "models/gemini-2.5-flash-native-audio-preview-12-2025",
      "generation_config": {
        "response_modalities": ["AUDIO"],
        "speech_config": {"voice_config": {"prebuilt_voice_config": {"voice_name": "Aoede"}}}
      },
      "system_instruction": {"parts": [{"text": "..."}]},
      "tools": [{"function_declarations": [...]}],
      "output_audio_transcription": {}
    }
  }

  This looks correct. The output_audio_transcription: {} enables getting text transcripts of what the AI says, which
  your code already handles.

  Tool Calls Mid-Stream

  During a voice call, Gemini can issue tool calls:

  Client                              Gemini
    |<─── {"toolCall": {               |
    |        "functionCalls": [{        |
    |          "id": "...",             |
    |          "name": "add_ingredient",|
    |          "args": {...}            |
    |        }]                          |
    |      }}                            |
    |                                    |
    |──── {"toolResponse": {           |  (results sent back)
    |        "functionResponses": [{    |
    |          "id": "...",             |
    |          "name": "...",           |
    |          "response": {...}        |
    |        }]                          |
    |      }} ──────────────────────────>|
    |                                    |
    |<─── {"serverContent": {...}} ─────|  (AI responds based on tool result)

  Your handleToolCall and sendFunctionResponse look correct. The tool call format matches the API spec.

  Key protocol detail: Sending text during a call

  When the user types text during an active voice call, it goes through WebSocket as client_content:

  {
    "client_content": {
      "turns": [{"role": "user", "parts": [{"text": "..."}]}],
      "turn_complete": true
    }
  }

  Your code handles this correctly in sendText() — it checks isConnected and routes through WebSocket if active, REST
  otherwise.

  Potential protocol issue: Model name

  gemini-2.5-flash-native-audio-preview-12-2025 — check if this model is still available. Google frequently rotates
  preview model names. If the WebSocket connects but setupComplete never arrives, this could be why (the acceptance
  timeout would fire at 6s).

  ---
  Deep Dive 3: CallKit + AVAudioSession

  Current Flow

  User taps phone button
      ↓
  ChatView: callPresentationStyle = .fullScreen
      ↓
  CallView.onAppear → viewModel.startVoiceSession()
      ↓
  ├── callState.isPresented = true
  ├── liveActivityManager.startCallActivity()  ← STUB (no-op)
  ├── callKitManager?.startCall()
  │     ↓
  │     CXStartCallAction → system shows call in recents
  │     provider.reportOutgoingCall(startedConnectingAt:)
  │     ↓
  │     CXProviderDelegate.didActivate(audioSession:)
  │         ↓
  │         onStartAudio callback
  │             ↓
  │             configureAudioSessionForCall()  ← sets .playAndRecord, .voiceChat
  │             startAudioCapture()  ← starts AVAudioEngine
  │             callState.isListening = true
  │
  └── connect(mode: .audio)
        ↓
        GeminiService.connect() → WebSocket opens → setup message sent
        ↓
        setupComplete received → geminiServiceDidConnect()
            ↓
            flushPendingMessages()
            startCallTimer()
            callKitManager?.reportConnected()  ← system shows "connected"

  The CallKit Timing Problem

  There's a race condition: CallKit's didActivate(audioSession:) can fire before the WebSocket is connected. Your code
  handles this with pendingVoiceStart:

  if pendingVoiceStart, geminiService?.currentMode == .audio {
      if !callKitEnabled {  // ← BUG: this guard is wrong!
          startAudioCapture()
          callState.isListening = true
      }
      pendingVoiceStart = false
  }

  Bug: When callKitEnabled = true (the default), this block does nothing because of the !callKitEnabled guard. But when
  CallKit is enabled, audio capture was already started by the onStartAudio callback — so this is actually fine in the
  CallKit path. The problem is the non-CallKit fallback path: if callKitEnabled = false, audio capture starts in
  startVoiceSession() only if already connected, or waits for geminiServiceDidConnect with pendingVoiceStart = true —
  and then the guard !callKitEnabled correctly allows it.

  So this isn't actually buggy — it's just confusing. The real issue is the audio format bugs above.

  AVAudioSession Conflicts

  What GetStream/100ms handle that you don't: When CallKit activates the audio session, it may change the audio
  session's sample rate and I/O buffer duration. After didActivate, you should query the actual format:

  func provider(_ provider: CXProvider, didActivate audioSession: AVAudioSession) {
      // The system may have changed the sample rate
      let actualRate = audioSession.sampleRate  // Could be 8kHz, 16kHz, 48kHz
      // Configure your audio engine AFTER this callback
      onStartAudio?()
  }

  This means your AVAudioConverter should be created inside the capture start, not ahead of time, because the actual
  device format may differ from what you expect.

  Live Activity (Dynamic Island) — Currently a Stub

  LiveActivityManager is all TODOs. For the collapse/dismiss behavior to work properly (user dismisses call screen →
  Dynamic Island shows call), this needs to be implemented with ActivityKit. The reference SDKs all rely on this for
  audio-only PiP.

  What the correct end-call flow should look like

  User taps End
      ↓
  1. Show "Call Ended" overlay (1.5s)
  2. callKitManager?.endCall()  → CXEndCallAction
  3. CXProviderDelegate.endCallAction → onStopAudio → stopAudioCapture()
  4. CXProviderDelegate.didDeactivate → clean confirmation
  5. geminiService?.disconnect() → WebSocket closes
  6. liveActivityManager.endCallActivity() → Dynamic Island dismisses
  7. resetCallTimer()
  8. Dismiss call screen

  Currently the code does steps 2-8 all at once in stopVoiceSession(). The "Call Ended" overlay and the sequencing of
  CallKit → audio → WebSocket shutdown should be ordered.

  ---
  Deep Dive 4: Image/Attachment Pipeline

  The Broken PhotosPicker Flow

  ChatView.swift:47:
  .photosPicker(isPresented: $showPhotosPicker, selection: $selectedItem, matching: .any(of: [.images, .videos]))

  ChatView.swift:51:
  .onChange(of: selectedItem) { handleSelectedItemChange() }

  ChatView.swift:87-91:
  private func handleSelectedItemChange() {
      guard selectedItem != nil else { return }
      Task {
          selectedItem = nil  // ← Discards without loading!
      }
  }

  And in ChatAttachmentService.swift:31-56:
  /* static func loadFromPhotos(item: PhotosPickerItem) async throws -> ChatAttachment {
      // ... correctly loads image/video from PhotosPickerItem
  } */

  The method is commented out! The loadFromPhotos function exists but is commented out (lines 31-56). The
  handleSelectedItemChange should be calling it.

  The Fix

  private func handleSelectedItemChange() {
      guard let item = selectedItem else { return }
      selectedItem = nil
      Task {
          do {
              selectedAttachment = try await ChatAttachmentService.loadFromPhotos(item: item)
          } catch {
              print("Failed to load attachment: \(error)")
          }
      }
  }

  And uncomment loadFromPhotos in ChatAttachmentService.swift.

  Camera Photo/Video — Works

  CameraCapturePicker feeds directly into ChatAttachmentService.loadFromCameraImage() or loadFromCameraVideo() → these
  correctly create a ChatAttachment → which gets set as selectedAttachment → which gets passed to
  viewModel.sendMessage(text, attachment:).

  REST Path for Images — Works

  Once the attachment makes it to sendToGemini():
  - sendTextWithPhoto() → base64 encodes JPEG → sends as inline_data with mime_type: "image/jpeg" ✓
  - sendPhoto() → same pattern ✓
  - The REST body includes conversation history + system prompt + tools ✓

  WebSocket Path for Images During Call

  When in a call, images are sent via WebSocket client_content:
  {"client_content": {"turns": [{"role": "user", "parts": [{"inline_data": {"mime_type": "image/jpeg", "data":
  "base64..."}}]}], "turn_complete": true}}

  This looks correct per the API spec. But there's a question: does the audio model
  (gemini-2.5-flash-native-audio-preview) accept image inputs? Some audio preview models are audio-only. This could
  silently fail.

  Video Frames During Call

  CameraService captures frames at 5fps → JPEG → geminiService.sendVideoFrame() → sent as realtime_input media chunks
  with image/jpeg. This is the correct approach per the Live API docs for video streaming.

  ⎿  Wrote 209 lines to C:\Users\18312\Projects\chef-yes-chef\docs\rebuild\01-audio-pipeline.md
        1 # Audio Pipeline: End-to-End Deep Dive
        2
        3 ## Overview
        4
        5 The audio pipeline handles bidirectional voice communication between the user's microphone and Gemini L
          ive API. Audio flows in two directions:
        6 - **Capture**: Microphone → resample → PCM16 → base64 → WebSocket → Gemini
        7 - **Playback**: Gemini → WebSocket → base64 → PCM16 → AVAudioPlayerNode → speaker
        8
        9 ## Current State (Broken)
       10
       11 ### Bug A: Capture sends wrong sample rate
       12
       13 **File**: `app/Views/Chat/ChatViewModel.swift` lines 435-491
       14
       15 The capture tap uses `inputNode.outputFormat(forBus: 0)` which returns the **device's native sample rat
          e** (typically 44.1kHz or 48kHz). The `convertToPCM16()` function converts float32 → Int16 but **does n
          ot resample**. The WebSocket declares `audio/pcm;rate=16000`, so Gemini receives 48kHz audio labeled as
           16kHz — garbled input.
       16
       17 ```swift
       18 // Current (broken):
       19 let format = inputNode.outputFormat(forBus: 0)  // ← 44.1kHz or 48kHz
       20 inputNode.installTap(onBus: 0, bufferSize: 1024, format: format) { buffer, _ in
       21     self?.processAudioBuffer(buffer)
       22 }
       23
       24 // convertToPCM16 just clips float→Int16, no resampling:
       25 private func convertToPCM16(buffer: AVAudioPCMBuffer) -> Data {
       26     guard let channelData = buffer.floatChannelData?[0] else { return Data() }
       27     let frameLength = Int(buffer.frameLength)
       28     var pcmData = Data(capacity: frameLength * 2)
       29     for i in 0..<frameLength {
       30         let sample = Int16(max(-1, min(1, channelData[i])) * Float(Int16.max))
       31         withUnsafeBytes(of: sample.littleEndian) { pcmData.append(contentsOf: $0) }
       32     }
       33     return pcmData
       34 }
       35 ```
       36
       37 ### Bug B: Playback configured at wrong rate
       38
       39 **File**: `app/Views/Chat/ChatViewModel.swift` lines 531-551
       40
       41 Playback engine is configured at 16kHz but Gemini Live API returns audio at **24kHz**.
       42
       43 ```swift
       44 // Current (wrong rate):
       45 let format = AVAudioFormat(commonFormat: .pcmFormatInt16, sampleRate: 16_000, channels: 1, interleaved:
           false)
       46 ```
       47
       48 Playing 24kHz audio at 16kHz makes everything sound slow and distorted.
       49
       50 ## The Fix
       51
       52 ### Capture: Add AVAudioConverter for resampling
       53
       54 ```swift
       55 private var audioConverter: AVAudioConverter?
       56 private var targetFormat: AVAudioFormat?
       57
       58 private func startAudioCapture() {
       59     if audioEngine?.isRunning == true { return }
       60
       61     audioEngine = AVAudioEngine()
       62     guard let audioEngine = audioEngine else { return }
       63
       64     let inputNode = audioEngine.inputNode
       65     let inputFormat = inputNode.outputFormat(forBus: 0)
       66
       67     // Create target format: 16kHz, mono, Int16
       68     let target = AVAudioFormat(commonFormat: .pcmFormatInt16,
       69                                 sampleRate: 16000, channels: 1,
       70                                 interleaved: false)!
       71     targetFormat = target
       72     audioConverter = AVAudioConverter(from: inputFormat, to: target)
       73
       74     inputNode.installTap(onBus: 0, bufferSize: 1024, format: inputFormat) { [weak self] buffer, _ in
       75         self?.processAudioBuffer(buffer)
       76     }
       77
       78     do {
       79         try audioEngine.start()
       80     } catch {
       81         print("Audio Engine Start Error: \(error)")
       82     }
       83 }
       84 ```
       85
       86 ### Capture: Resample in processAudioBuffer
       87
       88 ```swift
       89 private func processAudioBuffer(_ buffer: AVAudioPCMBuffer) {
       90     guard let channelData = buffer.floatChannelData?[0] else { return }
       91     let frameLength = Int(buffer.frameLength)
       92     guard frameLength > 0 else { return }
       93
       94     // 1. Audio level for UI
       95     var sum: Float = 0
       96     for i in 0..<frameLength { sum += abs(channelData[i]) }
       97     let average = sum / Float(frameLength)
       98     Task { @MainActor in
       99         self.callState.audioLevel = min(1.0, average * 10)
      100     }
      101
      102     // 2. Resample to 16kHz PCM16 and send
      103     guard let converter = audioConverter, let target = targetFormat else { return }
      104     let ratio = target.sampleRate / buffer.format.sampleRate
      105     let capacity = UInt32(Double(buffer.frameLength) * ratio)
      106     guard capacity > 0,
      107           let convertedBuffer = AVAudioPCMBuffer(pcmFormat: target, frameCapacity: capacity) else { ret
          urn }
      108
      109     var error: NSError?
      110     var inputConsumed = false
      111     converter.convert(to: convertedBuffer, error: &error) { _, outStatus in
      112         if inputConsumed {
      113             outStatus.pointee = .noDataNow
      114             return nil
      115         }
      116         inputConsumed = true
      117         outStatus.pointee = .haveData
      118         return buffer
      119     }
      120
      121     if let error { print("Audio conversion error: \(error)"); return }
      122
      123     // Extract Int16 data from converted buffer
      124     let data = Data(bytes: convertedBuffer.int16ChannelData![0],
      125                     count: Int(convertedBuffer.frameLength) * 2)
      126     geminiService?.sendAudio(data: data)
      127 }
      128 ```
      129
      130 ### Playback: Fix sample rate to 24kHz
      131
      132 ```swift
      133 private func setupPlaybackEngineIfNeeded() {
      134     if playbackEngine != nil { return }
      135
      136     let engine = AVAudioEngine()
      137     let player = AVAudioPlayerNode()
      138     engine.attach(player)
      139
      140     // Gemini Live API outputs 24kHz PCM16 mono
      141     let format = AVAudioFormat(commonFormat: .pcmFormatInt16,
      142                                sampleRate: 24_000, channels: 1,
      143                                interleaved: false)
      144     engine.connect(player, to: engine.mainMixerNode, format: format)
      145
      146     do {
      147         try engine.start()
      148     } catch {
      149         print("Audio Playback Engine Error: \(error)")
      150         return
      151     }
      152
      153     playbackEngine = engine
      154     playbackNode = player
      155     playbackFormat = format
      156 }
      157 ```
      158
      159 ### Mute: Flag-based instead of engine restart
      160
      161 ```swift
      162 private var isMuted = false
      163
      164 func toggleMute() {
      165     isMuted.toggle()
      166     callState.isListening = !isMuted
      167     // Don't stop/start the engine — just skip sending packets
      168 }
      169
      170 private func processAudioBuffer(_ buffer: AVAudioPCMBuffer) {
      171     // Still compute audio level for UI even when muted
      172     // ...
      173
      174     guard !isMuted else { return }  // Skip sending when muted
      175
      176     // Resample and send...
      177 }
      178 ```
      179
      180 ## Reference SDK Patterns
      181
      182 ### swift-gemini-api
      183 - Uses `AVAudioConverter` for format conversion
      184 - Encapsulates PCM format specs to prevent rate mismatches
      185 - May batch audio frames to reduce WebSocket overhead
      186
      187 ### GetStream (stream-video-swift)
      188 - Uses `AVAudioConverter` for resampling between device and network formats
      189 - Maintains separate capture and playback engines
      190 - Handles audio route changes gracefully
      191
      192 ### LiveKit (client-sdk-swift)
      193 - `AudioManager` class controls audio engine lifecycle
      194 - Automatic `AVAudioSession` configuration (can be disabled for CallKit)
      195 - `AudioEngineObserver` chains for processing audio
      196
      197 ### 100ms (hms-roomkit-ios)
      198 - Automatic audio session management by default
      199 - Toggle methods: `toggleMic()`, `toggleCamera()`, `leaveSession()`
      200 - Audio session lifecycle tied to room state
      201
      202 ## Verification
      203
      204 After fixing:
      205 1. Start a voice call
      206 2. Speak — Gemini should understand you clearly (no garbled input)
      207 3. Gemini responds — audio should sound at normal speed/pitch (not slow)
      208 4. Mute toggle should be instant (no audio engine restart delay)
      209 5. Check audio levels UI still updates while muted

        1 # WebSocket Protocol: Gemini Live API Deep Dive
        2
        3 ## Overview
        4
        5 The Gemini Live API uses a bidirectional WebSocket for real-time audio streaming. The protocol has dist
          inct phases: setup, streaming, and tool calling.
        6
        7 ## Connection URL
        8
        9 ```
       10 wss://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/ws/google.ai.generativelanguage.v1beta.GenerativeService.BidiGe
          nerateContent?key=API_KEY
       11 ```
       12
       13 ## Protocol Flow
       14
       15 ### Phase 1: Setup Handshake
       16
       17 ```
       18 Client → Server:
       19 {
       20   "setup": {
       21     "model": "models/gemini-2.5-flash-native-audio-preview-12-2025",
       22     "generation_config": {
       23       "response_modalities": ["AUDIO"],
       24       "speech_config": {
       25         "voice_config": {
       26           "prebuilt_voice_config": {
       27             "voice_name": "Aoede"
       28           }
       29         }
       30       }
       31     },
       32     "system_instruction": {
       33       "parts": [{"text": "system prompt here"}]
       34     },
       35     "tools": [
       36       {"function_declarations": [...]}
       37     ],
       38     "output_audio_transcription": {}
       39   }
       40 }
       41
       42 Server → Client:
       43 {"setupComplete": {}}
       44 ```
       45
       46 **Available voices**: Aoede, Charon, Fenrir, Kore, Puck
       47
       48 **Current code** (GeminiService.swift:186-216): Structure is correct. The `output_audio_transcription:
          {}` key enables text transcription of AI audio output.
       49
       50 ### Phase 2: Audio Streaming
       51
       52 **Sending audio** (continuous, during call):
       53 ```json
       54 {
       55   "realtime_input": {
       56     "media_chunks": [
       57       {
       58         "mime_type": "audio/pcm;rate=16000",
       59         "data": "base64-encoded-PCM16-mono"
       60       }
       61     ]
       62   }
       63 }
       64 ```
       65
       66 **Sending text** (during call):
       67 ```json
       68 {
       69   "client_content": {
       70     "turns": [
       71       {
       72         "role": "user",
       73         "parts": [{"text": "message text"}]
       74       }
       75     ],
       76     "turn_complete": true
       77   }
       78 }
       79 ```
       80
       81 **Sending images** (during call):
       82 ```json
       83 {
       84   "client_content": {
       85     "turns": [
       86       {
       87         "role": "user",
       88         "parts": [
       89           {"text": "what's this?"},
       90           {"inline_data": {"mime_type": "image/jpeg", "data": "base64..."}}
       91         ]
       92       }
       93     ],
       94     "turn_complete": true
       95   }
       96 }
       97 ```
       98
       99 **Sending video frames** (live camera feed):
      100 ```json
      101 {
      102   "realtime_input": {
      103     "media_chunks": [
      104       {
      105         "mime_type": "image/jpeg",
      106         "data": "base64-jpeg-frame"
      107       }
      108     ]
      109   }
      110 }
      111 ```
      112
      113 ### Phase 3: Server Responses
      114
      115 **Input transcript** (what the user said — server-side STT):
      116 ```json
      117 {
      118   "serverContent": {
      119     "inputTranscript": "do I have any eggs left?"
      120   }
      121 }
      122 ```
      123
      124 **Model turn** (AI response — may contain audio, text, and transcript):
      125 ```json
      126 {
      127   "serverContent": {
      128     "modelTurn": {
      129       "parts": [
      130         {
      131           "inlineData": {
      132             "mime_type": "audio/pcm;rate=24000",
      133             "data": "base64-audio-chunk"
      134           }
      135         },
      136         {
      137           "transcript": "Just two left in the fridge, chef."
      138         }
      139       ]
      140     }
      141   }
      142 }
      143 ```
      144
      145 **Turn complete** (AI finished responding):
      146 ```json
      147 {
      148   "serverContent": {
      149     "turnComplete": true
      150   }
      151 }
      152 ```
      153
      154 ### Phase 4: Tool Calls
      155
      156 **Server requests a tool call**:
      157 ```json
      158 {
      159   "toolCall": {
      160     "functionCalls": [
      161       {
      162         "id": "call-id-123",
      163         "name": "add_ingredient",
      164         "args": {
      165           "name": "eggs",
      166           "quantity": 12,
      167           "unit": "count",
      168           "location": "fridge"
      169         }
      170       }
      171     ]
      172   }
      173 }
      174 ```
      175
      176 **Client sends tool result**:
      177 ```json
      178 {
      179   "toolResponse": {
      180     "functionResponses": [
      181       {
      182         "id": "call-id-123",
      183         "name": "add_ingredient",
      184         "response": {
      185           "success": true,
      186           "message": "Added 12 count of eggs to the fridge",
      187           "ingredient": {"name": "eggs", "quantity": 12, "unit": "count"}
      188         }
      189       }
      190     ]
      191   }
      192 }
      193 ```
      194
      195 ## Current Implementation Analysis
      196
      197 ### What's correct:
      198 - Setup message structure (GeminiService.swift:186-216) ✓
      199 - Audio send format (GeminiService.swift:283-300) ✓
      200 - Server content parsing (GeminiService.swift:691-771) ✓
      201 - Tool call handling (GeminiService.swift:775-810) ✓
      202 - Text/image send via WebSocket (GeminiService.swift:305-401) ✓
      203
      204 ### Potential issues:
      205
      206 1. **Model name**: `gemini-2.5-flash-native-audio-preview-12-2025` — Google rotates preview model names
           frequently. If setup never completes, this is the first thing to check.
      207
      208 2. **No reconnection backoff**: In `geminiServiceDidDisconnect`, the ViewModel immediately calls `conne
          ct()` again. Should use exponential backoff (1s, 2s, 4s, 8s, max 30s).
      209
      210 3. **Acceptance timeout at 6s**: May be too short for cold starts. Consider 10s.
      211
      212 4. **No ping/pong**: The WebSocket has no keep-alive mechanism. Apple's `URLSessionWebSocketTask` handl
          es TCP-level pings automatically, but application-level heartbeats aren't sent.
      213
      214 ### VAD (Voice Activity Detection)
      215
      216 The current implementation relies entirely on **server-side VAD** — Gemini decides when the user has st
          opped speaking. This works but can feel laggy.
      217
      218 **What swift-gemini-api adds**: Client-side VAD that detects silence and can pre-emptively signal turn
          completion. This makes conversations feel more responsive.
      219
      220 For now, server-side VAD is acceptable. Client-side VAD is an optimization for later.
      221
      222 ## Reference Patterns
      223
      224 ### swift-gemini-api
      225 - `GeminiLiveClient` wraps the WebSocket lifecycle
      226 - Handles setup/setupComplete handshake
      227 - Provides callbacks: `onAudioReceived`, `onTextReceived`, `onToolCall`
      228 - Manages VAD state
      229 - Auto-reconnection with backoff
      230
      231 ### pipecat-client-ios-gemini-live-websocket
      232 - Transport layer abstraction over the WebSocket
      233 - Can pipe audio through other services before hitting Gemini
      234 - More complex agentic workflow support
      235 - Not needed for direct Gemini communication
      236
      237 ## Recommended Improvements
      238
      239 1. **Exponential backoff for reconnection**:
      240 ```swift
      241 private var reconnectDelay: TimeInterval = 1.0
      242 private let maxReconnectDelay: TimeInterval = 30.0
      243
      244 func handleDisconnect() {
      245     if callState.isPresented {
      246         Task {
      247             try? await Task.sleep(nanoseconds: UInt64(reconnectDelay * 1_000_000_000))
      248             connect(mode: .audio)
      249             reconnectDelay = min(reconnectDelay * 2, maxReconnectDelay)
      250         }
      251     }
      252 }
      253
      254 // Reset on successful connection:
      255 func handleConnect() {
      256     reconnectDelay = 1.0
      257 }
      258 ```
      259
      260 2. **Verify model name on each release** — add a config constant that's easy to update.
      261
      262 3. **Consider increasing acceptance timeout** to 10s for reliability.
      263
      264 ## Verification
      265
      266 1. Start voice call → WebSocket connects → `setupComplete` received within 6-10s
      267 2. Speak → `inputTranscript` events appear (user's words)
      268 3. AI responds → `modelTurn` with `inlineData` (audio) and `transcript`
      269 4. `turnComplete` fires after AI finishes speaking
      270 5. Tool calls work: say "add eggs to my pantry" → tool call chip appears → result sent back → AI acknow
          ledges
      271 6. Disconnect WiFi → reconnection attempts with backoff → reconnects when network returns

        1 # CallKit + AVAudioSession: Deep Dive
        2
        3 ## Overview
        4
        5 For a native "phone call" experience, three Apple frameworks work together:
        6 - **AVAudioSession**: Configures the audio hardware (mic input, speaker output, routing)
        7 - **CallKit**: Integrates with the iOS system call UI (shows call in recents, interruption handling, mu
          te from Control Center)
        8 - **ActivityKit (Live Activity)**: Shows call status in Dynamic Island when the app is backgrounded
        9
       10 ## Current Implementation
       11
       12 ### AVAudioSession Setup
       13
       14 **File**: `ChatViewModel.swift` lines 149-157, 182-190
       15
       16 ```swift
       17 let session = AVAudioSession.sharedInstance()
       18 try session.setCategory(.playAndRecord, mode: .voiceChat, options: [.defaultToSpeaker, .allowBluetoothH
          FP])
       19 try session.setActive(true)
       20 ```
       21
       22 This is correct. The key options:
       23 - `.playAndRecord`: Enables simultaneous mic input and speaker output
       24 - `.voiceChat`: Optimizes for voice (reduces latency, enables echo cancellation)
       25 - `.defaultToSpeaker`: Routes to loudspeaker by default (FaceTime behavior)
       26 - `.allowBluetoothHFP`: Allows Bluetooth headsets (HFP profile for calls)
       27
       28 ### Speakerphone Toggle
       29
       30 **File**: `ChatViewModel.swift` lines 192-199
       31
       32 ```swift
       33 private func preferSpeaker() {
       34     try session.overrideOutputAudioPort(.speaker)
       35 }
       36 ```
       37
       38 To toggle back to earpiece:
       39 ```swift
       40 try session.overrideOutputAudioPort(.none)  // Routes to earpiece
       41 ```
       42
       43 Currently `preferSpeaker()` is called once at connection time but there's no toggle exposed to the UI.
          The `AudioRoutePickerView` wraps `AVRoutePickerView` which shows the system audio route picker — this h
          andles speaker/Bluetooth/earpiece selection natively.
       44
       45 ### CallKit Integration
       46
       47 **File**: `app/Services/CallKitManager.swift`
       48
       49 The implementation is minimal but correct:
       50
       51 ```
       52 startCall() → CXStartCallAction → system registers call
       53                                  → didActivate(audioSession:) callback
       54                                      → onStartAudio closure fires
       55                                          → configureAudioSessionForCall()
       56                                          → startAudioCapture()
       57
       58 endCall() → CXEndCallAction → system deregisters call
       59                              → didDeactivate(audioSession:) callback
       60                                  → onStopAudio closure fires
       61                                      → stopAudioCapture()
       62
       63 Mute from Control Center → CXSetMutedCallAction
       64                           → onMuteChanged(isMuted) callback
       65 ```
       66
       67 ### What's Missing
       68
       69 1. **`reportConnected()` timing**: Currently called in `geminiServiceDidConnect()`. This is correct — i
          t tells iOS the outgoing call was answered, which updates the system UI from "Calling..." to the connec
          ted state.
       70
       71 2. **Incoming call support**: Not applicable (AI doesn't initiate calls), but `CXProviderConfiguration.
          supportsVideo = false` is set.
       72
       73 3. **Call interruption**: The `handleInterruption()` method handles system interruptions (e.g., real ph
          one call comes in). When `.began`, it stops audio capture. When `.ended` with `.shouldResume`, it resta
          rts. This is correct.
       74
       75 4. **Live Activity**: `LiveActivityManager` is all stubs. Without this, there's no Dynamic Island prese
          nce when the user backgrounds the app during a call.
       76
       77 ## The Call Lifecycle (How It Should Work)
       78
       79 ### Starting a Call
       80
       81 ```
       82 1. User taps phone icon in nav bar
       83 2. ChatView: callPresentationStyle = .fullScreen
       84 3. CallView appears → .onAppear triggers startVoiceSession()
       85 4. startVoiceSession():
       86    a. callState.isPresented = true
       87    b. liveActivityManager.startCallActivity()  → Dynamic Island appears
       88    c. callKitManager.startCall() → System registers outgoing call
       89    d. connect(mode: .audio) → WebSocket connection begins
       90 5. CallKit: didActivate(audioSession:) fires → onStartAudio callback
       91    a. configureAudioSessionForCall() → AVAudioSession configured
       92    b. startAudioCapture() → AVAudioEngine starts, tap installed
       93    c. callState.isListening = true
       94 6. WebSocket: setupComplete received → geminiServiceDidConnect()
       95    a. connectionState = .connected
       96    b. startCallTimer()
       97    c. callKitManager.reportConnected() → System shows "connected"
       98    d. flushPendingMessages()
       99 7. Audio flows bidirectionally
      100 ```
      101
      102 ### During a Call
      103
      104 ```
      105 User speaks → AVAudioEngine tap → resample → WebSocket → Gemini
      106 Gemini responds → WebSocket → audio data → AVAudioPlayerNode → speaker
      107 User toggles mute → isMuted flag → audio packets stop/resume
      108 User changes audio route → AVRoutePickerView → system handles routing
      109 App backgrounded → Dynamic Island shows call status
      110 Dynamic Island tapped → app foregrounded, call screen shown
      111 ```
      112
      113 ### Ending a Call
      114
      115 ```
      116 1. User taps End button
      117 2. Show "Call Ended" overlay (1.5s)
      118 3. stopVoiceSession():
      119    a. callState.isPresented = false
      120    b. liveActivityManager.endCallActivity() → Dynamic Island dismisses
      121    c. callKitManager.endCall() → CXEndCallAction
      122    d. CallKit: didDeactivate(audioSession:) → onStopAudio → stopAudioCapture()
      123    e. geminiService.disconnect() → WebSocket closes
      124    f. resetCallTimer()
      125 4. Dismiss call screen
      126 ```
      127
      128 ### Dismissing Without Ending (Audio-Only)
      129
      130 For audio calls, when the user swipes down or navigates away:
      131 - The call continues in the background
      132 - Dynamic Island shows call indicator with duration
      133 - Tapping Dynamic Island returns to call screen
      134 - This requires ActivityKit implementation (currently stubbed)
      135
      136 ## CallKit + AVAudioSession Interaction
      137
      138 ### Critical: AVAudioSession is owned by CallKit during a call
      139
      140 When CallKit is active, **CallKit owns the audio session**. This means:
      141 - You should NOT call `setCategory()` or `setActive()` yourself
      142 - Wait for `didActivate(audioSession:)` before starting your audio engine
      143 - The system may change the sample rate — always check after activation
      144
      145 ```swift
      146 func provider(_ provider: CXProvider, didActivate audioSession: AVAudioSession) {
      147     // The system activated the audio session — NOW start your engine
      148     // The sample rate may have changed from what you expected
      149     let actualRate = audioSession.sampleRate
      150     print("Activated with sample rate: \(actualRate)")
      151     onStartAudio?()
      152 }
      153 ```
      154
      155 ### What GetStream/100ms do
      156
      157 Both SDKs:
      158 1. Disable automatic audio session configuration when CallKit is used
      159 2. Let CallKit manage the audio session lifecycle
      160 3. Create their audio engine AFTER `didActivate` fires
      161 4. Destroy their audio engine on `didDeactivate`
      162
      163 ### Route Change Handling
      164
      165 ```swift
      166 // Already implemented in ChatViewModel.observeAudioSession()
      167 // Watches AVAudioSession.routeChangeNotification
      168 // Updates callState.isListening based on output availability
      169 ```
      170
      171 This is correct but could be enhanced to detect specific route changes (Bluetooth connected/disconnecte
          d, headphones plugged/unplugged).
      172
      173 ## Live Activity (Dynamic Island) — TODO
      174
      175 **File**: `app/Services/LiveActivityManager.swift` — All stubs
      176
      177 Needs ActivityKit implementation:
      178 1. Define an `ActivityAttributes` struct for call state
      179 2. Start activity when call begins (shows in Dynamic Island)
      180 3. Update with call duration every second
      181 4. End activity when call ends
      182 5. Handle tap gesture to return to call screen
      183
      184 This is required for the "dismiss call screen but keep calling" behavior.
      185
      186 ## Reference Patterns
      187
      188 ### GetStream
      189 - CallKit integration built into their `Call` object
      190 - Audio session management through `AudioSessionManager`
      191 - Automatic handling of interruptions and route changes
      192
      193 ### 100ms
      194 - Audio session auto-configured by default
      195 - Can be disabled for manual CallKit control
      196 - `toggleMic()` and `toggleCamera()` as simple state toggles
      197
      198 ### LiveKit
      199 - `AudioManager.shared.audioSession.isAutomaticConfigurationEnabled = false` for CallKit
      200 - `AudioEngineObserver` chains for audio processing
      201 - Separate audio session lifecycle from video
      202
      203 ## Verification
      204
      205 1. Start call → appears in system call log (Recents tab in Phone app)
      206 2. During call, open Control Center → mute button works → syncs with app UI
      207 3. Real phone call comes in → call is interrupted → resumes after
      208 4. Bluetooth headset connects during call → audio routes to headset
      209 5. (After Live Activity) Background app → Dynamic Island shows call → tap returns

        3 ## Overview
        4
        5 The app supports sending images, videos, and documents to Gemini. There are multiple input sources (Pho
          tosPicker, camera, document picker) and two delivery paths (REST API for text mode, WebSocket for call
          mode).

       12 - Document picker → `ChatAttachmentService.loadFromDocument()` → attachment → REST send ✓

       86 ## Complete Attachment Flow (After Fix)
       87
       88 ### Input Sources
       89
       90 ```
       91 PhotosPicker → .onChange(of: selectedItem) → handleSelectedItemChange()
       92                                             → ChatAttachmentService.loadFromPhotos(item:)
       93                                             → selectedAttachment = ChatAttachment
       94
       95 Camera Photo → CameraCapturePicker(mode: .photo) → ChatAttachmentService.loadFromCameraImage(_:)
       96                                                    → selectedAttachment = ChatAttachment
       97
       98 Camera Video → CameraCapturePicker(mode: .video) → ChatAttachmentService.loadFromCameraVideo(_:)
       99                                                    → selectedAttachment = ChatAttachment
      100
      101 Document     → DocumentPicker → handleDocumentSelection(_:)
      102                                → ChatAttachmentService.loadFromDocument(url:)
      103                                → selectedAttachment = ChatAttachment
      104 ```
      105
      106 ### Sending (all sources converge here)
      107
      108 ```
      109 User taps Send
      110     ↓
      111 ChatView.onSend: viewModel.sendMessage(text, attachment: selectedAttachment)
      112     ↓
      113 ChatViewModel.sendMessage():
      114     buildMessage(text:, attachment:) → ChatMessage with imageData, mediaType, etc.
      115     insertMessage() → SwiftData persistence
      116     messages.append() → UI update
      117     enqueueOrSend() → routes to appropriate path
      118     ↓
      119     ┌─ Not in call → sendToGemini() → REST path
      120     │   ├─ text + image → sendTextWithPhotoREST() → base64 JPEG inline_data
      121     │   ├─ image only  → sendPhotoREST() → base64 JPEG inline_data
      122     │   ├─ text only   → sendTextREST() → text parts
      123     │   └─ video/doc   → sendVideoAttachment()/sendDocumentAttachment() → STUB (not supported)
      124     │
      125     └─ In call (WebSocket connected) → sendToGemini() → WebSocket path
      126         ├─ text + image → sendTextWithPhoto() → client_content with text + inline_data parts
      127         ├─ image only  → sendPhoto() → client_content with inline_data part
      128         ├─ text only   → sendText() → client_content with text part
      129         └─ video/doc   → sendVideoAttachment()/sendDocumentAttachment() → STUB
      130 ```
      131
      132 ### REST API Path (text mode)
      133
      134 ```json
      135 POST /v1beta/models/gemini-2.5-flash:generateContent
      136
      137 {
      138   "contents": [
      139     ...conversationHistory,
      140     {
      141       "role": "user",

      146     }

      150 }
      151 ```

      153 ### WebSocket Path (during call)
      154
      155 ```json
      156 {
      157   "client_content": {
      158     "turns": [{
      159       "role": "user",
      160       "parts": [
      161         {"text": "what's this ingredient?"},
      162         {"inline_data": {"mime_type": "image/jpeg", "data": "base64..."}}
      163       ]
      164     }],
      165     "turn_complete": true
      166   }
      167 }
      168 ```

      170 ## Image Processing
      171
      172 ### Compression & Resizing
      173
      174 `CameraService.processImageForGemini()` handles optimization:
      175 - Max size: 1024x1024 pixels
      176 - JPEG compression: 0.8 quality
      177 - Preserves aspect ratio
      178
      179 For PhotosPicker images, the raw `Data` from `loadTransferable` is used directly. Consider adding the s
          ame processing:
      180
      181 ```swift
      182 static func loadFromPhotos(item: PhotosPickerItem) async throws -> ChatAttachment {
      183     // ... load data ...
      184     // Optionally resize/compress for consistency:
      185     if let uiImage = UIImage(data: data) {
      186         let processed = processForGemini(uiImage)
      187         return ChatAttachment(kind: .image, imageData: processed, ...)
      188     }
      189 }
      190 ```
      191
      192 ## Multimodal During Voice Call — Caveat
      193
      194 When sending images via WebSocket during a voice call, the audio model (`gemini-2.5-flash-native-audio-
          preview`) may or may not support image inputs. This depends on the specific model version. If images ar
          e silently ignored during calls, this is a model limitation, not a code bug.
      195
      196 **Video frames** sent via `realtime_input` media chunks ARE supported by the Live API for vision-capabl
          e models.
      197
      198 ## Video/Document Attachments — Not Yet Supported
      199
      200 `sendVideoAttachment()` and `sendDocumentAttachment()` are stubs:
      201 ```swift
      202 func sendVideoAttachment(url: URL, utType: String?) {
      203     guard isConnected else { return }
      204     guard supportsFileAttachments else { return }  // ← always false
      205     // TODO
      206 }
      207 ```
      208
      209 The Gemini REST API supports file uploads via the File API, but this isn't implemented yet. For now, vi
          deos and documents can be displayed locally but aren't sent to Gemini.

       COMPLETE AUDIO PIPELINE ANALYSIS - swift-gemini-api

       Based on my thorough exploration of the swift-gemini-api repository, here is the COMPLETE audio pipeline
       documentation:

       FILE STRUCTURE

       Core Audio Files (in /Sources/swift-gemini-api/):
       - AudioRecorder.swift - Microphone input capture & resampling
       - StreamingAudioPlayer.swift - Audio playback engine
       - GeminiLiveClient.swift - WebSocket client & audio stream management

       ---
       1. AUDIO CAPTURE & RESAMPLING (AudioRecorder.swift)

       Setup Phase:
       public final class AudioRecorder: ObservableObject, AudioRecorderProtocol
       - @Published var isRecording: Bool
       - var onChunk: ((String) -> Void)?  // Base64 chunks callback
       - var inputUnit: AudioUnit?
       - var audioConverter: AudioConverterRef?

       AudioUnit Configuration:
       - On iOS: Uses kAudioUnitSubType_RemoteIO
       - On macOS: Uses kAudioUnitSubType_HALOutput
       - Enables Input IO on Bus 1, disables Output IO on Bus 0
       - Device: Default system input device

       Sample Rate Detection:
       func getDeviceSampleRate(deviceID: AudioDeviceID) -> Double?
       - Queries device's nominal sample rate (typically 44100 or 48000 Hz on real devices)
       - Falls back to 44100 if query fails

       Native Input Format:
       streamFormat = AudioStreamBasicDescription(
           mSampleRate: sampleRate,           // Device native (44100/48000)
           mFormatID: kAudioFormatLinearPCM,
           mFormatFlags: kAudioFormatFlagIsSignedInteger | kAudioFormatFlagIsPacked,
           mBytesPerPacket: 2,
           mFramesPerPacket: 1,
           mBytesPerFrame: 2,
           mChannelsPerFrame: 1,              // MONO
           mBitsPerChannel: 16,               // 16-bit signed PCM
           mReserved: 0
       )

       Target Format (For Sending to Gemini):
       func getDestFormat() -> AudioStreamBasicDescription {
           AudioStreamBasicDescription(
               mSampleRate: 16000,            // FIXED AT 16kHz
               mFormatID: kAudioFormatLinearPCM,
               mFormatFlags: kAudioFormatFlagIsSignedInteger | kAudioFormatFlagIsPacked,
               mBytesPerPacket: 2,
               mFramesPerPacket: 1,
               mBytesPerFrame: 2,
               mChannelsPerFrame: 1,          // MONO
               mBitsPerChannel: 16,           // 16-bit signed PCM
               mReserved: 0
           )
       }

       AudioConverter Setup:
       var sourceFormat = streamFormat           // Native device format
       var destFormat = getDestFormat()           // 16kHz target
       var converter: AudioConverterRef?
       let converterStatus = AudioConverterNew(&sourceFormat, &destFormat, &converter)
       self.audioConverter = converter

       Input Callback Flow:
       private func inputCallback(
           inRefCon: UnsafeMutableRawPointer,
           ioActionFlags: UnsafeMutablePointer<AudioUnitRenderActionFlags>,
           inTimeStamp: UnsafePointer<AudioTimeStamp>,
           inBusNumber: UInt32,
           inNumberFrames: UInt32,
           ioData: UnsafeMutablePointer<AudioBufferList>?
       ) -> OSStatus

       Steps in callback:
       1. Extract AudioRecorder from refCon
       2. Call AudioUnitRender() to fill bufferList
       3. Write to ExtAudioFile (original format)
       4. Call convertTo16kHz() for resampling
       5. Base64 encode converted data
       6. Invoke onChunk(base64String) callback

       Resampling Implementation:
       func convertTo16kHz(inputData: UnsafeRawPointer, inputFrames: UInt32) -> Data?
       - Uses AudioConverterFillComplexBuffer()
       - Input: Raw PCM at device native rate + frame count
       - Output callback: audioConverterInputProc provides input buffer
       - Returns: Data with resampled 16-bit PCM at 16kHz

       func audioConverterInputProc(
           inAudioConverter: AudioConverterRef,
           ioNumberDataPackets: UnsafeMutablePointer<UInt32>,
           ioData: UnsafeMutablePointer<AudioBufferList>,
           outDataPacketDescription: UnsafeMutablePointer<UnsafeMutablePointer<AudioStreamPacketDescription>?>?,
           inUserData: UnsafeMutableRawPointer?
       ) -> OSStatus
       - Provides the input buffer list to converter
       - Sets packet count based on buffer size / bytes per frame

       2. SENDING AUDIO VIA WEBSOCKET (GeminiLiveClient.swift)

       WebSocket Client Setup:
       private var socket: URLSessionWebSocketTask?
       private var urlSession: URLSession?
       private let audioDataChunks = AudioDataBuffer()

       public func connect(apiKey: String?) {
           let socket = urlSession!.webSocketTask(with: url)
           self.socket = socket
           socket.resume()
           listen()
       }

       URL Format:
       wss://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/ws/google.ai.generativelanguage.v1alpha.GenerativeService.BidiGenera
       teContent?key={apiKey}

       Sending Audio Chunks (from Recorder):
       public func sendAudio(base64: String) {
           if mute { return }

           let message: [String: Any] = [
               "realtimeInput": [
                   "mediaChunks": [
                       [
                           "data": base64,
                           "mimeType": "audio/pcm;rate=16000"
                       ]
                   ]
               ]
           ]

           Task {
               if await self.setup.didComplete() {
                   self.send(json: message)
               }
           }
       }

       Key Details:
       - Chunks are wrapped individually in mediaChunks array
       - MIME type: "audio/pcm;rate=16000"
       - Data must be base64 encoded
       - Only sent if setup is complete
       - Mute flag can prevent sending

       Sending Audio Data (Alternative Overload):
       public func sendAudio(
           data: Data,
           sampleRate: Int = 24000,
           bitDepth: Int = 16,
           channels: Int = 1,
           silenceSeconds: Int = 1
       ) {
           // Appends silence after audio for natural turn-taking
           let bytesPerSample = bitDepth / 8
           let silenceByteCount = sampleRate * bytesPerSample * channels * silenceSeconds
           let silenceData = Data(repeating: 0, count: silenceByteCount)
           let dataWithSilence = data + silenceData
           let base64 = dataWithSilence.base64EncodedString()

           // Same message structure as above
       }

       Setup Message (First Message on Connect):
       private func sendSetup() {
           let setup: [String: Any] = [
               "model": "models/gemini-live-2.5-flash-preview",
               "generationConfig": [
                   "candidateCount": 1,
                   "maxOutputTokens": 1024,
                   "temperature": 0.7,
                   "topP": 1,
                   "topK": 0,
                   "response_modalities": ["AUDIO"],
                   "speech_config": [
                       "voice_config": [
                           "prebuilt_voice_config": ["voice_name": "Kore"]  // Configurable
                       ],
                       "language_code": "en-US"  // Configurable
                   ]
               ],
               "systemInstruction": [
                   "parts": [["text": systemPrompt]]
               ],
               "realtime_input_config": [
                   "automaticActivityDetection": [
                       "disabled": false,
                       "start_of_speech_sensitivity": "START_SENSITIVITY_HIGH",
                       "end_of_speech_sensitivity": "END_SENSITIVITY_HIGH",
                       "prefix_padding_ms": 20,
                       "silence_duration_ms": 100
                   ]
               ],

                   "functionDeclarations": [],

               "input_audio_transcription": [:]    // Optional

       ---
       3. RECEIVING & PLAYING AUDIO (GeminiLiveClient + StreamingAudioPlayer)

       Audio Data Reception:
       private func onData(_ data: Data) {
           // Parse JSON response
           if let serverContent = jsonObject["serverContent"] as? [String: Any] {
               if let modelTurn = serverContent["modelTurn"] as? [String: Any],
                  let parts = modelTurn["parts"] as? [[String: Any]] {

                   for part in parts {
                       if let inlineData = part["inlineData"] as? [String: Any],
                          let base64 = inlineData["data"] as? String,
                          let data = Data(base64Encoded: base64) {

                           // Store in buffer
                           await self.audioDataChunks.append(data)

                           // Enqueue for playback
                           if playAudio {
                               self.audioPlayer.enqueue(data)
                           }
                       }
                   }
               }
           }
       }

       Audio Format from Gemini:
       - Encoded in "inlineData" with base64 encoding
       - Embedded in "modelTurn"."parts"[].inlineData.data"
       - Decoded to PCM data on receipt

       Streaming Audio Player:
       class StreamingAudioPlayer {
           private let audioEngine = AVAudioEngine()
           private let playerNode = AVAudioPlayerNode()
           private let sampleRate: Double = 24000  // GEMINI OUTPUT RATE
           private let channels: AVAudioChannelCount = 1  // MONO

           // Format used internally
           let format = AVAudioFormat(
               commonFormat: .pcmFormatFloat32,
               sampleRate: 24000,
               channels: 1,
               interleaved: false
           )
       }

       Playback Pipeline:
       1. Incoming base64 decoded to Data
       2. Data passed to enqueue(data)
       3. Conversion from Int16 to Float32 for AVAudioEngine
       4. Scheduled on AVAudioPlayerNode
       5. Playback via speakers

       func scheduleBuffer(_ data: Data) {
           let frameCount = UInt32(data.count) / 2  // 16-bit = 2 bytes per frame

           guard let buffer = AVAudioPCMBuffer(pcmFormat: audioFormat, frameCapacity: frameCount) else {
               return
           }

           buffer.frameLength = frameCount

           // Convert Int16 -> Float32
           data.withUnsafeBytes { rawBufferPointer in
               let int16Pointer = rawBufferPointer.bindMemory(to: Int16.self)
               let floatChannelData = buffer.floatChannelData![0]

               for i in 0..<Int(frameCount) {
                   floatChannelData[i] = Float(int16Pointer[i]) / Float(Int16.max)
               }
           }

           playerNode.scheduleBuffer(buffer, completionHandler: nil)

           if !isPlaying {
               playerNode.play()
               isPlaying = true
           }
       }

       AVAudioSession Setup:
       #if os(iOS)
           try AVAudioSession.sharedInstance().setCategory(.playback, mode: .default, options: .mixWithOthers)
           try AVAudioSession.sharedInstance().setActive(true)
       #endif

       ---
       4. AUDIO BUFFERING & FILE WRITING

       Chunk Buffering Actor:
       public actor AudioDataBuffer {
           private var chunks: [Data] = []

           func append(_ data: Data) { chunks.append(data) }
           func reduce(_ combine: ([Data]) -> Data) -> Data { combine(chunks) }
           func removeAll() { chunks.removeAll() }
           func snapshot() -> [Data] { chunks }
       }

       WAV File Writing on Completion:
       private func writeAudioToWAV() async {
           let pcmData = await audioDataChunks.reduce { chunks in
               chunks.reduce(Data(), +)  // Concatenate all chunks
           }
           let wavData = createWAVFile(from: pcmData)

           // Write to documents directory
           let outputURL = urls[0].appendingPathComponent("gemini_live_response_\(timestamp()).wav")
           try wavData.write(to: outputURL)

           await audioDataChunks.removeAll()
       }

       WAV File Creation (from VoiceUtils.swift):
       func createWAVFile(from pcmData: Data) -> Data {
           let sampleRate: UInt32 = 24_000  // Gemini output rate
           let bitsPerSample: UInt32 = 16
           let numChannels: UInt32 = 1

           // Build WAV header manually
           var header = Data()
           header.append("RIFF".data(using: .ascii)!)
           header.append(UInt32(chunkSize).littleEndianData)
           header.append("WAVE".data(using: .ascii)!)
           // ... fmt chunk ...
           // ... data chunk ...

           return header + pcmData
       }

       ---
       5. UTILITY FUNCTIONS & HELPERS

       Voice Activity Detection (VAD):
       func hasSpeech(in pcmData: Data, sampleRate: Int = 16000, threshold: Float = 0.01) -> Bool {
           let samples = pcmData.withUnsafeBytes {
               Array(UnsafeBufferPointer<Int16>(
                   start: $0.baseAddress!.assumingMemoryBound(to: Int16.self),
                   count: pcmData.count / MemoryLayout<Int16>.size
               ))
           }

           let energy = samples.reduce(0.0) { sum, sample in
               let normalized = Float(sample) / Float(Int16.max)
               return sum + normalized * normalized
           } / Float(samples.count)

           return energy > threshold  // Default threshold: 0.01
       }

       PCM to Base64 Encoding:
       func base64EncodeBuffer(_ buffer: AVAudioPCMBuffer) -> String? {
           guard let int16ChannelData = buffer.int16ChannelData else { return nil }

           let channelData = int16ChannelData[0]
           let dataSize = Int(buffer.frameLength) * MemoryLayout<Int16>.size
           let audioData = Data(bytes: channelData, count: dataSize)

           return audioData.base64EncodedString()
       }

       PCM Format Conversion (AVAudioConverter):
       func convertBufferTo16kMonoPCM(_ buffer: AVAudioPCMBuffer) throws -> AVAudioPCMBuffer {
           guard let targetFormat = AVAudioFormat(
               commonFormat: .pcmFormatInt16,
               sampleRate: 16_000,
               channels: 1,
               interleaved: true
           ) else { throw ... }

           guard let converter = AVAudioConverter(from: buffer.format, to: targetFormat) else { throw ... }

           let ratio = targetFormat.sampleRate / buffer.format.sampleRate
           let outCapacity = AVAudioFrameCount(Double(buffer.frameLength) * ratio)

           guard let outBuffer = AVAudioPCMBuffer(pcmFormat: targetFormat, frameCapacity: outCapacity) else { throw
        ... }

           try converter.convert(to: outBuffer, from: buffer)
           return outBuffer
       }

       Timestamp Generation:
       func timestamp() -> String {
           let dateFormatter = DateFormatter()
           dateFormatter.dateFormat = "yyyyMMdd_HHmmss"
           return dateFormatter.string(from: Date())
       }

       ---
       6. END-TO-END USAGE EXAMPLE (LiveView.swift)

       Initialization:
       @ObservedObject var recorder = AudioRecorder()
       @State private var client: GeminiLiveClient?

       .onAppear() {
           client = GeminiLiveClient(
               onSetupComplete: self.onSetupComplete,
               verbose: false,
               input_audio_transcription: false,
               output_audio_transcription: false
           )

           recorder.setOnChunk { chunk in
               client?.sendAudio(base64: chunk)
           }
       }

       Connection Flow:
       Button("Start Gemini Live Session") {
           client?.setOutputTranscription { transcription in
               print("Output: \(transcription)")
           }

           client?.connect(apiKey: apiKey!)
       }

       Recording:
       Button(action: {
           if recorder.isRecording {
               recorder.stopRecording()
           } else {
               recorder.startRecording()
           }
       }) {
           Text(recorder.isRecording ? "Stop Recording" : "Start Recording")
       }

       Sending Synthetic Audio:
       func sayToGeminiLive(_ text: String) async throws {
           let speech = GeminiSpeech(apiKey: apiKey!)
           let pcmData = try await speech.synthesizeSpeech(text)
           client?.sendAudio(data: pcmData)
       }

       ---
       7. FRAMEWORK DEPENDENCIES

       Package.swift:
       platforms: [
           .iOS(.v14),
           .macOS(.v15)
       ],
       linkerSettings: [
           .linkedFramework("AudioToolbox"),     // Low-level audio APIs
           .linkedFramework("AVFoundation"),     // Audio session
           .linkedFramework("AVFAudio")          // AVAudioEngine, AVAudioPlayerNode
       ]

       8. KEY TECHNICAL DECISIONS

       ┌────────────────────┬──────────────────────────┬─────────────────────────────────────────────┐
       │      Feature       │         Decision         │                   Details                   │
       ├────────────────────┼──────────────────────────┼─────────────────────────────────────────────┤
       │ Input Sample Rate  │ Device-adaptive          │ Detects 44100/48000, converts to 16kHz      │
       ├────────────────────┼──────────────────────────┼─────────────────────────────────────────────┤
       │ Output Sample Rate │ 24000 Hz                 │ Gemini streams at 24kHz                     │
       ├────────────────────┼──────────────────────────┼─────────────────────────────────────────────┤
       │ Format             │ 16-bit PCM               │ Signed, mono, little-endian                 │
       ├────────────────────┼──────────────────────────┼─────────────────────────────────────────────┤
       │ Channels           │ Mono                     │ Single channel throughout                   │
       ├────────────────────┼──────────────────────────┼─────────────────────────────────────────────┤
       │ Encoding Over WS   │ Base64                   │ Each chunk base64 encoded separately        │
       ├────────────────────┼──────────────────────────┼─────────────────────────────────────────────┤
       │ Turn-Taking        │ Manual + Silence padding │ Can add silence after audio blocks          │
       ├────────────────────┼──────────────────────────┼─────────────────────────────────────────────┤
       │ Mute Control       │ Global flag              │ Prevents sending in sendAudio()             │
       ├────────────────────┼──────────────────────────┼─────────────────────────────────────────────┤
       │ Playback           │ Float32 internally       │ Converts Int16 -> Float32 for AVAudioEngine │
       ├────────────────────┼──────────────────────────┼─────────────────────────────────────────────┤
       │ Audio Buffering    │ Actor-based              │ Thread-safe chunk accumulation              │
       ├────────────────────┼──────────────────────────┼─────────────────────────────────────────────┤
       │ Devices            │ Default input/output     │ System handles device selection             │
       └────────────────────┴──────────────────────────┴─────────────────────────────────────────────┘

       ---
       CRITICAL AUDIO PIPELINE PATTERNS

       Capture Flow:
       Microphone (device native rate)
           ↓ [AudioUnit.RemoteIO]
           ↓ [Input Callback + AudioUnitRender]
           ↓ [AudioConverterFillComplexBuffer: native → 16kHz]
           ↓ [Base64 encode]
           ↓ [onChunk callback]
           ↓ [WebSocket: audio/pcm;rate=16000]
           ↓ GeminiLiveClient

       Playback Flow:
       GeminiLiveClient (receives base64)
           ↓ [Base64 decode]
           ↓ [AudioDataBuffer accumulate]
           ↓ [StreamingAudioPlayer.enqueue]
           ↓ [Int16 → Float32 conversion]
           ↓ [AVAudioPCMBuffer create]
           ↓ [AVAudioPlayerNode.scheduleBuffer]
           ↓ [Speakers (24kHz sample rate)]

       File Write Flow:
       Audio chunks collected in AudioDataBuffer
           ↓ [On generationComplete]
           ↓ [Concatenate all chunks]
           ↓ [Wrap in WAV header (24kHz)]
           ↓ [Write to documents/gemini_live_response_*.wav]
           ↓ [Clear buffer]

       Audio Engine Patterns Report: GetStream vs Pipecat iOS SDKs

       Based on deep code exploration of both repositories, here's the actual implementation code for audio engine
       patterns:

       PIPECAT iOS (Gemini Live WebSocket)

       1. Audio Format Configuration

       AudioCommon.swift - Central audio configuration:
       enum AudioCommon {
           static var serverAudioFormat: AVAudioFormat = {
               AVAudioFormat(commonFormat: .pcmFormatInt16, sampleRate: 24000, channels: 1, interleaved: false)!
           }()

           static let audioLevelReportingRate = 10

           static func installAudioLevelTap(onNode node: AVAudioNode, callback: @escaping (Float) -> ()) {
               let format = node.outputFormat(forBus: 0)
               let rate = format.sampleRate
               let bufferSize = rate / Double(audioLevelReportingRate)
               node.installTap(
                   onBus: 0,
                   bufferSize: AVAudioFrameCount(bufferSize),
                   format: format) { buffer, _ in
                       callback(calculateRMSAudioLevel(fromBuffer: buffer))
                   }
           }

           static func calculateRMSAudioLevel(fromBuffer buffer: AVAudioPCMBuffer) -> Float {
               let channelData = buffer.floatChannelData![0] // assumes 1 channel and float
               let frameLength = Int(buffer.frameLength)
               var sum: Float = 0.0
               for frame in 0..<frameLength {
                   sum += channelData[frame] * channelData[frame]
               }
               let meanSquare = sum / Float(frameLength)
               let rms = sqrt(meanSquare)
               return rms
           }
       }

       Key format: PCM Int16, 24kHz mono, non-interleaved

       2. Audio Recording (Capture) - AudioRecorder.swift

       class AudioRecorder {
           var isRecording: Bool {
               audioEngine.isRunning
           }

           func resume() throws {
               // Setup the audio engine for recording
               audioEngine = AVAudioEngine()
               try audioEngine.inputNode.setVoiceProcessingEnabled(true) // ignores output from phone
               let inputNode = audioEngine.inputNode
               let inputFormat = inputNode.inputFormat(forBus: 0)

               // Create converter from input format to target format
               let formatConverter = AVAudioConverter(
                   from: inputFormat,
                   to: AudioCommon.serverAudioFormat
               )!

               // Install tap for recording
               audioEngine.inputNode.installTap(
                   onBus: 0,
                   bufferSize: UInt32(AudioCommon.serverAudioFormat.sampleRate) /
       UInt32(AudioCommon.audioLevelReportingRate),
                   format: inputFormat
               ) { [weak self] inputBuffer, time in
                   guard let self else { return }

                   // Report audio level
                   var audioLevel = AudioCommon.calculateRMSAudioLevel(fromBuffer: inputBuffer)
                   audioLevel = min(1, audioLevel * 10)
                   delegate?.audioRecorder(self, didGetAudioLevel: audioLevel)

                   // Convert captured buffer to target format
                   let targetBuffer = Self.convertToTargetFormat(
                       inputBuffer: inputBuffer,
                       inputFormat: inputFormat,
                       targetFormat: AudioCommon.serverAudioFormat,
                       formatConverter: formatConverter)

                   // Convert buffer to data
                   let channels = UnsafeBufferPointer(
                       start: targetBuffer.int16ChannelData,
                       count: Int(targetBuffer.format.channelCount)
                   )
                   let data = NSData(
                       bytes: channels[0],
                       length: Int(targetBuffer.frameLength *
       targetBuffer.format.streamDescription.pointee.mBytesPerFrame)
                   )

                   streamAudioContinuation?.yield(data as Data)
               }

               try audioEngine.start()
               didSetup = true
           }

           private static func convertToTargetFormat(
               inputBuffer: AVAudioPCMBuffer,
               inputFormat: AVAudioFormat,
               targetFormat: AVAudioFormat,
               formatConverter: AVAudioConverter) -> AVAudioPCMBuffer
           {
               let targetBuffer = AVAudioPCMBuffer(
                   pcmFormat: targetFormat,
                   frameCapacity: inputBuffer.frameLength
               )!
               var error: NSError?
               var inputIndex: AVAudioFramePosition = 0

               formatConverter.convert(
                   to: targetBuffer,
                   error: &error) { numberOfFrames, inputStatus in
                       if (inputIndex >= inputBuffer.frameLength) {
                           inputStatus.pointee = .noDataNow
                           return AVAudioBuffer()
                       }
                       inputStatus.pointee = .haveData
                       let startFrame = inputIndex
                       let endFrame = min(
                           inputIndex + Int64(numberOfFrames),
                           AVAudioFramePosition(inputBuffer.frameLength)
                       )
                       inputIndex = endFrame
                       let segment = segment(of: inputBuffer, from: startFrame, to: endFrame)
                       return segment
                   }

               // Fix frameLength set by converter (appears to be a quirk)
               targetBuffer.frameLength = inputBuffer.frameLength
               if let error {
                   Logger.shared.warn("Error converting raw mic audio data: \(error)")
               }
               return targetBuffer
           }

           func pause() {
               audioEngine.pause()
           }

           func stop() {
               if !didSetup { return }
               audioEngine.inputNode.removeTap(onBus: 0)
               audioEngine.stop()
               didSetup = false
           }
       }

       Key capture points:
       - setVoiceProcessingEnabled(true) - Enables voice processing to ignore speaker output
       - installTap with buffer size = sampleRate / 10 (for 10 Hz reporting)
       - AVAudioConverter used with input buffer provider callback pattern
       - PCM conversion: Takes float input, outputs Int16 at 24kHz
       - Data extraction: Uses int16ChannelData pointer and mBytesPerFrame for raw byte copying

       3. Audio Playback - AudioPlayer.swift

       class AudioPlayer {
           private var audioEngine: AVAudioEngine
           private var playerNode: AVAudioPlayerNode
           private let inputAudioFormat: AVAudioFormat
           private let playerAudioFormat: AVAudioFormat
           private let inputToPlayerAudioConverter: AVAudioConverter

           init() {
               audioEngine = AVAudioEngine()
               playerNode = AVAudioPlayerNode()
               inputAudioFormat = AudioCommon.serverAudioFormat
               playerAudioFormat = AVAudioFormat(
                   standardFormatWithSampleRate: inputAudioFormat.sampleRate,
                   channels: inputAudioFormat.channelCount
               )!
               inputToPlayerAudioConverter = AVAudioConverter(from: inputAudioFormat, to: playerAudioFormat)!
           }

           func start() throws {
               audioEngine = AVAudioEngine()
               playerNode = AVAudioPlayerNode()
               audioEngine.attach(playerNode)
               audioEngine.connect(
                   playerNode,
                   to: audioEngine.mainMixerNode,
                   format: playerAudioFormat
               )

               // Install tap to compute audio level
               AudioCommon.installAudioLevelTap(onNode: playerNode) { [weak self] audioLevel in
                   guard let self else { return }
                   delegate?.audioPlayer(self, didGetAudioLevel: audioLevel)
               }

               try audioEngine.start()
               playerNode.play()
               isRunning = true
           }

           func enqueueBytes(_ bytes: Data) {
               if !isRunning { return }
               if isRunning && !audioEngine.isRunning {
                   // Hard reset on Bluetooth disconnect issues
                   try? adaptToDeviceChange()
               }

               // Prepare input buffer from raw bytes
               let inputBuffer = AVAudioPCMBuffer(
                   pcmFormat: inputAudioFormat,
                   frameCapacity: UInt32(bytes.count) / inputAudioFormat.streamDescription.pointee.mBytesPerFrame
               )!
               inputBuffer.frameLength = inputBuffer.frameCapacity
               let channels = UnsafeBufferPointer(
                   start: inputBuffer.int16ChannelData,
                   count: Int(inputBuffer.format.channelCount)
               )
               (bytes as NSData).getBytes(UnsafeMutableRawPointer(channels[0]), length: bytes.count)

               // Convert to player-ready buffer
               let playerBuffer = AVAudioPCMBuffer(
                   pcmFormat: playerAudioFormat,
                   frameCapacity: inputBuffer.frameCapacity
               )!
               try! inputToPlayerAudioConverter.convert(to: playerBuffer, from: inputBuffer)

               // Schedule for playing
               playerNode.scheduleBuffer(playerBuffer, completionCallbackType: .dataPlayedBack) { [weak self]
       callbackType in
                   if callbackType == .dataPlayedBack {
                       self?.decrementEnqueuedBufferCount()
                   }
               }
               incrementEnqueuedBufferCount()
           }

           func stop() {
               if !isRunning { return }
               AudioCommon.uninstallAudioLevelTap(onNode: playerNode)
               playerNode.stop()
               enqueuedBufferCount = 0
               audioEngine.stop()
               isRunning = false
           }
       }

       Key playback points:
       - Engine created fresh on start()
       - playerNode attached to mainMixerNode
       - AVAudioConverter converts from server format (Int16) to playback format
       - Bytes → Buffer: Creates PCM buffer from raw Data, copies to int16ChannelData
       - Completion callbacks track when buffers finish playing
